function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 149') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.149!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

// Dir added: plugins/database
@mkdir('plugins/database');
if (!is_dir('plugins/database')) {
	warn('Directory could not be created: plugins/database');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database', 0755)) {
	warn('Could not change directory permissions of plugins/database');
}

// File added: plugins/database/index.html
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('plugins/database/index.html', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode(''));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('plugins/database/index.html') && (sha1_file('plugins/database/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/index.html');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/index.html');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/index.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/database/index.html', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('plugins/database/index.html')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/index.html');
} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/index.html');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/index.html', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/index.html');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'db95f3f7bbc7566052016ac32e7733cd75543f17') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'db95f3f7bbc7566052016ac32e7733cd75543f17') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'd7552907d640b29b5d186628ce205448c693f79b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'db95f3f7bbc7566052016ac32e7733cd75543f17') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/generate_wellknown_other');
	writefile_15();
	if (!is_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/generate_wellknown_other');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other') != '310b57ebf9e47c521831bf4c1b0b7d6f63ca204a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/generate_wellknown_other', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/generate_wellknown_other');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other') !== '310b57ebf9e47c521831bf4c1b0b7d6f63ca204a') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other') !== '23d3191a98af3c9ca666a0420795afafae6acae7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/generate_wellknown_other') !== '310b57ebf9e47c521831bf4c1b0b7d6f63ca204a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/generate_wellknown_other');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_24();

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php') != '10c13f56bb701c50bcc5f85b03a72f3be3c64451') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php');

	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php') !== '10c13f56bb701c50bcc5f85b03a72f3be3c64451') {

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php', $backup_name)) {

		writefile_24();

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_29();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != 'e3e06dca03f72d47f5ae72524c8e370fd805a08a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'e3e06dca03f72d47f5ae72524c8e370fd805a08a') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '0182d3c8336d6924813cd3bfec57ccd65be2258d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_29();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'e3e06dca03f72d47f5ae72524c8e370fd805a08a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_52();
	if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php') != '3bacefa388ccdd901f99d269d8c7a40f0d9693c4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php') !== '3bacefa388ccdd901f99d269d8c7a40f0d9693c4') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php') !== '058f16b91ed07bae6adc92da93b92bef36a001cc') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_52();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php') !== '3bacefa388ccdd901f99d269d8c7a40f0d9693c4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/093_rainfo/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php') != '7a87bf8041386877920793ffea630da39a5199b8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php') !== '7a87bf8041386877920793ffea630da39a5199b8') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php') !== '0b818275691dc7735fef6c1a45a91204cf21283f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_59();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php') !== '7a87bf8041386877920793ffea630da39a5199b8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/setup.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/setup.js');
	writefile_63();
	if (!is_file('setup/setup.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup.js') != '211235ed01514b0db27c54cb698757cdb7be9396') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.js') !== '211235ed01514b0db27c54cb698757cdb7be9396') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.js') !== '9155878752e63edc704ba155c3898e19d9444e42') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/setup.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_63();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.js') !== '211235ed01514b0db27c54cb698757cdb7be9396') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.js');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/struct.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/struct.sql') != 'de575ab034c23b80138dcebcf228e1bbdc96e423') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/struct.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/struct.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct.sql') !== 'de575ab034c23b80138dcebcf228e1bbdc96e423') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct.sql') !== 'cd1b490192dd0490a63908b3b0967300ea4f5afb') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/struct.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/struct.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/struct.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/struct.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_64();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct.sql') !== 'de575ab034c23b80138dcebcf228e1bbdc96e423') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct.sql');
		}
	}
}
